[Venus, Mars, and Moon in Horary]
Venus: 7 in the night. Mars: a participant day and night is the Moon. Table of houses, exaltations, falls, and triplicities of the planets. Day 1901.1. I. 3. 0.n. 174 15 1 Co.n. n. 0.n. 114 0.1 b210.7 1863 1281 15 27 1 19 b21 8 bn. 28 ho. 1 170 15 b 1 ha Dd ba b m X 1170 n.i Dd 120834 Ba 12 11 18/0 227151201 Did De of movable, fixed, and common signs. Four of these signs are said to be movable, namely Aries, Cancer, Libra, and Capricorn. And four fixed, namely Taurus, Leo, Scorpio, and Aquarius. The remaining four, namely Gemini, Virgo, Sagittarius, and Pisces, are common. They are called movable, fixed, or common because when the Sun enters any of them, the time moves, i.e., changes, or is fixed, i.e., perseveres in the same state, or becomes common, i.e., half of that one time will be as half of the other. For example, when the Sun enters the sign of Aries, the time changes, that is, winter turns into spring. And when it enters Taurus, the vernal time is fixed. But when the Sun enters Gemini, the time becomes common, i.e., half spring and half summer, and so on for the others. Concerning the aspects of the planets. Signs are also said to aspect each other: that is, every sign aspects the third before it and the third after it, which is the eleventh, and this aspect is called fertile and is an aspect of love and medium friendship, and it is also called sextile because it holds the sixth part of the circle, i.e., 60 degrees. For example, a planet that is at the beginning of Aries aspects that which is in Gemini before it and that which is in Aquarius after it, which is an aspect of friendship. And it aspects the fourth before it and the fourth after it, i.e., the tenth, and this aspect is called tetragonal because it holds the fourth part of the sky, i.e., 90 degrees, and it is an aspect of discord and medium enmity. And it also aspects the fifth sign before it and the fifth after it, which is the ninth, and this aspect is called trine or trine radiation because it holds the third part of the sky, i.e., 120 degrees, and it is an aspect of perfect concord and love. It aspects the seventh by opposition, and it is an aspect of perfect enmity. And if planets are in these signs thus aspecting each other, they are said to aspect each other; this is an aspect. And if two planets are in one sign, they are said to be conjoined. When a planet is in some sign, its rays will be in those signs that aspect that sign in a similar degree and minute. For example, if Mars is in the first degree of Aries and in the first minute of that degree, its rays will be in the first degree of the sign of Libra and in the first minute of that degree. Understand this for the other aspects as is most clearly shown in this figure.

[Planets in Signs and Body Parts]
In Taurus, Saturn rules the belly, Jupiter the back, Mars the neck, Sol the knees, Venus the head, Mercury the feet, Luna the legs. In Gemini, Saturn rules the belly, Jupiter the genitals and what follows them, Mars the chest and what follows it, Sol the legs and ankles (that is, the heels), Venus the neck, Mercury the head, Luna the thighs. In Cancer, Saturn rules the genitals and all that follows them, Jupiter the thighs, Mars the chest, Sol the feet, Venus the arms and shoulders, Mercury the eyes and throat, Luna the head. In Leo, Saturn rules the genitals and what follows them, Jupiter the thighs and knees, Mars the belly, Sol the head, Venus the heart, Mercury the shoulders and throat, Luna the neck. In Virgo, Saturn rules the feet, Jupiter the knees and what follows them, Mars the belly, Sol the neck, Venus the belly, Mercury the heart, Luna the shoulders. In Libra, Saturn rules the knees and what follows them, Jupiter the eyes and what follows them (that is, parts of the head), Mars the genitals and what follows them, Sol the shoulders, Venus the head, Mercury the belly, Luna the neck. In Scorpio, Saturn rules the ankles (that is, the heels) and what follows them, Jupiter the feet, Mars the head, arms, and thighs, Sol the neck, Venus the genitals and what follows them, Mercury the nose, Luna the belly. In Sagittarius, Saturn rules the feet, Jupiter the legs and head, Mars the feet and hands, Sol the belly, Venus the thighs and arms, Mercury the genitals and heart, Luna the back. In Capricorn, Saturn rules the head and feet, Jupiter the knees and eyes, Mars the legs and shoulders, Sol the back, Venus the thighs and heart, Mercury the genitals and what follows them, Luna the thighs. In Aquarius, Saturn rules the head and neck, Jupiter the shoulders, chest, and feet, Mars the ankles and heart, Sol the genitals and what follows them, Venus the knees and what follows them, Mercury the thighs and neck, Luna the genitals. In Pisces, Saturn rules the shoulders, arms, and neck, Jupiter the heart and head, Mars the ankles and belly, Sol the thighs and what follows them, Venus the neck and back, Mercury the legs and genitals, Luna the thighs. Concerning the masculine and feminine degrees of the signs. There are also in each sign degrees which are properly called masculine and feminine. For from the beginning of Aries up to the 8th degree they are said to be masculine; and from the 7th to the 9th, feminine; and from the 9th to the 15th, masculine; and from the 15th up to the 22nd, feminine; and from the 22nd up to the end of Aries, masculine. We have decided to describe these as we described the terms, and here we depict a table so that the work may be more easily understood, with God's help. 1 masculine, 8 feminine, 1 masculine, 6 feminine, 7 masculine, 8 feminine, 5 masculine, 6 feminine, 6 masculine, 4 feminine, 3 masculine, 0 feminine, 5 masculine, 3 feminine, 6 masculine, 4 feminine, 4 masculine, 2 feminine, 6 masculine, 2 feminine, 2 masculine, 11 feminine, 4 masculine, 3 masculine, 8 masculine, 5 feminine, 3 masculine, 7 feminine, 8 masculine, 7 feminine, 8 masculine, 4 feminine, 8 masculine, 10 masculine, 5 feminine, 10 masculine, 5 feminine, 7 masculine, 3 masculine, 4 feminine, 10 masculine, 3 feminine, 8 masculine, 5 masculine, 2 feminine, 3 masculine, 7 feminine, 12 masculine, 6 masculine, 11 feminine, 8 masculine, 11 masculine, 5 feminine, 10 masculine, 6 feminine, 4 masculine, 2 feminine, 3 masculine, 10 masculine, 10 feminine, 10 masculine, 3 feminine, 5 masculine, 2. Concerning the lucid, dark, smoky, and empty degrees. In each of these signs there are degrees which are called lucid, and degrees which are called dark, and degrees which are called smoky, and degrees which are called empty. For some say that from the beginning of Aries up to the third degree they are dark; and from the 3rd to the 8th, lucid; and from the 8th to the 16th, dark; and from the 16th to the 20th, lucid; and from the 20th up to the 24th, empty; and from the 23rd up to the 28th, lucid; and from the 29th to the end of Aries, empty. We will make a table of these, if God wills.

1 masculine, 8 feminine, 1 masculine, 6 feminine, 7 masculine, 8 feminine, 5 masculine, 6 feminine, 6 masculine, 4 feminine, 3 masculine, 0 feminine, 5 masculine, 3 feminine, 6 masculine, 4 feminine, 4 masculine, 2 feminine, 6 masculine, 2 feminine, 2 masculine, 11 feminine, 4 masculine, 3 masculine, 8 masculine, 5 feminine, 3 masculine, 7 feminine, 8 masculine, 7 feminine, 8 masculine, 4 feminine, 8 masculine, 10 masculine, 5 feminine, 10 masculine, 5 feminine, 7 masculine, 3 masculine, 4 feminine, 10 masculine, 3 feminine, 8 masculine, 5 masculine, 2 feminine, 3 masculine, 7 feminine, 12 masculine, 6 masculine, 11 feminine, 8 masculine, 11 masculine, 5 feminine, 10 masculine, 6 feminine, 4 masculine, 2 feminine, 3 masculine, 10 masculine, 10 feminine, 10 masculine, 3 feminine, 5 masculine, 2.

[Lucid, Dark, Smoky, and Empty Degrees]
In each of these signs there are degrees which are called lucid, and degrees which are called dark, and degrees which are called smoky, and degrees which are called empty. For some say that from the beginning of Aries up to the third degree they are dark; and from the 3rd to the 8th, lucid; and from the 8th to the 16th, dark; and from the 16th to the 20th, lucid; and from the 20th up to the 24th, empty; and from the 23rd up to the 28th, lucid; and from the 29th to the end of Aries, empty. We will make a table of these, if God wills.

[The Twelfth House]
The twelfth house is of enemies, labor, sadness, envy, whispering, cunning, ingenuity, and beasts. It signifies the end of life and what happens to mothers in their conception, whether good or bad. Alendezgod said that the lord of the triplicity of the house of enemies: the first signifies enemies, the second labors, and the third beasts and cattle. These are what the twelve houses signify. Concerning the colors of the twelve houses: The twelve houses also signify colors, and these are: the first house, the ascendant, and the seventh are white. The second and twelfth are green. The third and eleventh are yellow. The fourth and tenth are red. The fifth and eighth are honey-colored, that is, the color of honey. The sixth and ninth are black. Concerning the joys of the planets in the houses: Each planet has in one of these houses a certain power from the accidental powers, which are called joy: Mercury rejoices in the ascendant. The Moon in the third house. Venus also in the fifth. Mars in the sixth. The Sun in the eighth. Jupiter in the eleventh. Saturn in the twelfth. Concerning the strength of the angles: It is said that in the significations of the houses, the angles signify strength and perfection. Those falling from the angles, however, signify weakness and detriment. The eighth and fourth signify a suitable and revealed thing with fame. The twelfth and sixth signify concealment, retention, and the vileness of things. The angles and the lords of the angles signify the magnitude of good things, of price, and of fortune; strength, exercise, and elongation from the cause. Their presence in the cadent houses is contrary to fortune, that is, disgrace and fall. Concerning those succeeding the angles: The house succeeding the tenth, that is, the eleventh, signifies medium strength and fortune through friends, and from that part in which there was trust. And that which follows the fourth, that is, the fifth, signifies medium fortune through gifts and venerations and with children, with veneration, joy, and gladness. That which succeeds the ascendant, which is the second, similarly signifies medium fortune from the cause of substance and ministers. That which succeeds the seventh, that is, the eighth, similarly signifies medium fortune from inheritance, that is, from what is inherited from the dead and from hidden things. Concerning the significations of the lords of the angles: These are the significations of the lords of the angles when they are present in the angles. The presence of the lord of the ascendant in the ascendant signifies fortune for himself, and through his acquisition. And his presence in the tenth signifies kingship and higher magistracies. And when he is in the seventh, through conventions and agents and your things, through the presence of those whom he signifies in the fourth, fortune, inheritances, and the causes of fathers, through the production of waters and populations or plantations, that is, buildings, and from ancient and radical things. The lord of the tenth also signifies, through his presence in the tenth, fortune either through the king or through a great kingdom and higher magistracies. And his presence in the seventh signifies a kingdom through the victory of contentions and from the causes of wives. And through his presence in the fourth, he signifies a kingdom through the friendship of nobles and his king, and through the causes of tribunes, and through the dispensers of kings and the cultivation of lands and the building of cities, and through the divisions of rivers and the guardianship of cities, and from ancient things. And through his presence in the ascendant, he signifies kingdoms through ingenuity and through the proximity of the king to the things of the common people. The presence of the lord of the seventh in the seventh signifies fortune through negotiations and through conventions, and also through nourishments and women, and through agents. And his presence in the fourth signifies through the conventions of women, and through negotiations, and through the causes of fathers and inheritances and the cultivation of land. And his presence in the ascendant signifies through conventions and negotiations.

[Significations of Venus]
of waters, from the measure of water and also of earth; and from the quality of the soul, it signifies generosity and modesty and justice, and from sects, plurality and simulation. Some, however, have said that it signifies the liver and stomach and the left ear, arms and belly, and the lower parts of the pelvis and intestines, and from colors, the color of ashes and green and similar ones; and from tastes, sweetness; and the quantity of its orb is 9 degrees. And from days, Thursday; from nights, the night of Monday; and its fridaria years, that is, its dominion, are 12; and its maximum years are 428, major are 79, medium are 45 and a half, minor are 12; and its strength from the regions of the circle is in the west. And Masha'allah said that among men it signifies a white man having redness in his face, having eyes not entirely black, nostrils not equal and short, bald, having some blackness in his teeth, of beautiful stature, good spirit, good morals, beautiful body. And Dorotheus said that it signifies a man having large eyes, and a wide pupil, a curly beard; and it has from regions Alchirath, Babylonia, Asen, and Persia, and Alarames and Arcadia; and from parts, it has the part of perfect habit; and it signifies faith and appetite for good; and from works, health, security, and participation.

[Significations of Mars]
Mars is masculine, nocturnal, and evil; it produces heat and dryness; and it is the significator of brothers and peregrinations; and it has from ages youth up to the end of youth; and its nature is choleric, of a bitter taste; and from crafts, every fiery craft and what is done by iron and fire, such as the striking of swords with hammers. And if Saturn is conjoined with it, it signifies the striking of iron. If Jupiter, it signifies the striking of brass. If the Sun, it signifies the striking of gold coins. If Venus, it signifies the craft of ornaments. If Mercury, the striking of needles. If the Moon, it signifies the striking of book covers; it also signifies, when alone, the signification of the work of medicine. If no planet is conjoined with it, it signifies diminution, and wounding, and aptitude, and similar things. And if Saturn is conjoined with it, it signifies the work of medicine and wounds. And if Jupiter, it signifies the work of natures. And if the Sun, it signifies the care of eyes. If Venus, it signifies the work of ornament, such as cutting hair and beards and trimming nails; and if Mercury, it signifies the cutting of veins. If the Moon, it signifies the eradication of teeth and the cleansing of ears. And by itself, it signifies the injuries of the miserable, and the shedding of blood, and oppressions by force, and the cutting off of roads, and anger, and the leadership of an army, and haste, and shamelessness, and peregrination outside the homeland, and the foulness of coitus, the falling of children, that is, abortions, middle brothers and sisters, knowledge and discretion in the care of animals. And from illnesses, hot and bloody fevers, and bloody pustules, alabraba which is redness of the body with roughness and foulness and consumption of flesh with putrefaction; and half a headache; and sacred fire, and fear and horrible thoughts that disturb men and move and impede and render them empty; whatever is with inflammation of heat. And from the quality of the soul, namely, emotional disturbance and perturbation. If Saturn aspects it, it signifies hatred and great envy; and from sects, that in which there is war and unity and swiftness of change of faith; and a multitude of desires and change from testament to testament; all these will be under unity. Some have said that it has from the members the gall, kidneys, and veins, and the flow of semen and urine; it has from colors redness; and from tastes bitterness; and the quantity of its orb is 8 degrees. And from days, Tuesday; and from nights, the night of Saturday. Its fridaria years are seven; and its maximum years are 264, major are 66, medium are 40 and a half, minor are 15; and its strength in the regions of the circle is in the south. And Masha'allah said that it signifies among the images of men a red man having reddish hair and a round face, slightly dishonest, having yellowish eyes, of a bold appearance, audacious, having a mark or stain on his foot. And Dorotheus said that it signifies one having a sharp gaze; and from parts, the part of audacity; and it signifies perseverance, cunning, and pride, and lightness, and mobility, and audacity, and negotiation, sharpness, and haste in all things; and it has from the parts of the world Asia and the lands of the Romans up to the west, and the lands of the Tuscans.

[Significations of the Sun]
The Sun is fortunate by aspect, and evil by conjunction in one sign; and it is masculine, diurnal; it produces heat and dryness; and it is the significator of fathers. If the nativity is in the day, it signifies the greatest kingdom and a vital soul and light and splendor and intellect and beauty and cleanliness and faith. And from age, the end of youth. And it participates with all planets in the disposition of years. And from crafts, governance and principality; and it signifies the throwing of javelins and hunting, purification with every kind of cleansing by which bodies are purified internally and externally. And from illnesses, it signifies hot and dry illnesses appearing in bodies. And from substance, much gold and all kinds of substance. And from the quality of the soul itself, sublimity, prudence, and it follows honesty, that is, generosity and glory; and length of mind. And from sects, good culture and similar things. And it signifies the power of voice and the strength of swiftness. If Saturn is conjoined with it, it signifies stewardship and such principality. If Jupiter, it signifies principality in faith and religion and also a judge judging among men the works of oppressors or injuries, etc. If Mars, it signifies the leadership of an army and the investigation of wars. If Venus, it signifies a kingdom through women and through the obedience of the powerful. If Mercury, it signifies the counselors of kings and the work of books and inheritances and greater works. If the Moon, it signifies the work of legates and the detection of counsels and similar things. And some have said that the Sun signifies the image of a man's face; and specifically, in men, the right eye; in women, the left eye. And some have said that it has the brain and marrow and thighs. And from illnesses, the consumption of flesh in the mouth; and the detriment of all property; and the descent of water into the eye; its part in the head. And the Indians said that when it is in the ascendant, it will be burning and will have a mark on the face. And it has from colors whatever appears of a foreign color; and from tastes, sourness. And the quantity of its orb is 15 degrees. And from days, it has Sunday; and from nights, the night of Thursday. Its fridaria years are ten. And its major years are 120, maximum are 460, medium are 39 and a half, or according to some, 69 and a half; minor are 19. Its strength from the regions of the circle is in the east. And Masha'allah said that it signifies among the figures of men him who has a color between yellowish and black, that is, dark, covered with redness, of short stature, curly, bald, of beautiful body; and it has from tastes sharpness. And Dorotheus said that the figure of the Sun and Moon is the figure of the planets that are with them or of that which is more dignified in their place. Therefore, if you wish to know the figure of the Sun, know that it is yellowish, having a part of redness in the hair, its eyes somewhat yellowish. And from parts, having a part of future things, that is, a part of divination; and it is the significator of natures and the spirit of wisdom, elevation, and perfection of faith, also of sciences and praises. And from the parts of the world, it has Samarkand and Cura and Serit and its territories and the lands of the Romans. Leborus, Lelilad, F.

[Significations of the Planets]
If it is Fortune itself, Venus signifies courtesy and kindness, and a gentle spirit, and honest customs, and swiftness of movement, and divine obedience. If it is Jupiter, it signifies honesty, caution, and companionship, and kindness, and beauty of life. And if it is afflicted by malefics and it is Mars, it signifies a tendency to whisper among men and to use such things. If Saturn, hatred, simulation, and envy. If the Sun is in a praiseworthy aspect, it signifies a royal disposition. And if it is Mercury, it signifies rhetoric, that is, eloquence and goodness of tongue and writing. And some have said that it signifies thought and novelty of mind and weakness of sense and heaviness of tongue, and honest women, the nourishment of infants, and mothers and maternal aunts, and the preparation of foods. And others have said that it properly signifies the brain and the lung. And from colors it has saffron, and from tastes, salt. And the quantity of its orb is 12 degrees. And it signifies the left eye in men, and the right in women. And from days it has Monday, and from nights, the night of Venus. Its Firdaria years are nine, or 105 major, 520 maximum, and 66 and a half medium, and according to some, 39 and a half, and 25 minor. And its strength from the regions of the circle is to the right of the west. And Masha'allah said that among the figures of men, it signifies a white man tinged with redness, with joined eyebrows, benevolent, having eyes not entirely black, a round beautiful stature, and a mark on his face. And from earthly things it has artichoke and tinamou and alder. And some have said that it signifies childhood from the beginning of the month up to 7 days; from 7 days up to 14 days, youth; and it signifies the age of perfection, that is, middle age up to 21 days and nights; and old age up to conjunction, that is, up to the end of the month when it is conjoined with the Sun. And when it is under the Sun's rays, it signifies secrets and hidden things; and similarly every planet. And at the beginning of the month when it increases, it signifies everything that is to be done; and at its fullness, what is to be destroyed, because it decreases. And at the beginning of the month, it and the Sun signify accusers; and at the end of the month, the accused. And at the beginning of the month, it signifies gain and continence; at the end of the month, stipends and dispersions. And in opposition, it signifies contrariety. And at the beginning of the change to opposition, that is, when there are 15 degrees between it and the opposition, it signifies the beginning of contrariety and its cause. And when it has separated from opposition, it signifies the causes of exception from contrariety. And in its exit from under the Sun's rays, it signifies exit from concealment and its daughter. And in its entrance under the rays, it signifies adaptation to concealment. And the hour of its division from the Sun signifies its aptative exit from concealment. And the hour of its exit from under the rays signifies appearance, arrival from absence. And when it is in the fourth aspect of the Sun, it signifies diminution of a thing or descent from high to low. Similarly in the fourth aspect, but in the first fourth aspect, it signifies the appearance of things and gain and increase of continence; and in the second fourth aspect of the Sun, it signifies the opposite of these. And some have said that from the conjunction up to the first half of its light, its nature will be humid; and from the middle of its light up to its fullness, its nature will be hot; from its fullness up to the second half of its light, its nature will be dry; and from the second half of its light up to the conjunction, its nature will be cold. The other planets, from their rising up to their first station, will be in the nature of humidity and signify childhood; and from their first station up to the opposition of the Sun, their nature will be hot and signify youth; and from this place up to the second station, their nature will be dry and signify perfect age; and from their second station up to their first occultation, their nature will be cold and signify cold old age. And some have said that the Sun signifies the spirit, that is, the vital soul. The Moon, thought and sense. Saturn, melancholy and sadness, vitality and evil. Jupiter, wisdom and reason. Mars, anger, fury, and swiftness. Venus, play and joy. Mercury, rationality or dialectic and discipline. And because we have spoken in this chapter about the signification of the planets when they are conjoined with another planet, similarly it must be considered in other things that the planets signify. Regarding the order of the planets or their rulership when in the conception of children, when they have been in the mother's womb, it must be known that the first month from the hour of conception is of Saturn. The second of Jupiter. The third of Mars. The fourth of the Sun. The fifth of Venus. The sixth of Mercury. The seventh of the Moon. The eighth of Saturn; and therefore he who is born in the eighth month does not live, because he is born under the power of Saturn. And the ninth of Jupiter. The rulership or order of the planets in human life, that is, how they dispose the life of the native, is divided thus: The Moon begins from the native's entrance, that is, from the birth of the child, and disposes the quantity of nourishing years, which are four years. Then Mercury for ten, then Venus for eight. Afterwards the Sun for nineteen. Afterwards Mars for fifteen. Afterwards Jupiter for twelve. Then Saturn up to the end of life. Regarding the nature of the Dragon's Head and Tail. The Dragon's Head is masculine. Similarly, it is also fortune, and its nature is composed of the nature of Jupiter and Venus; and this signifies kingdom and fortune and substance. And some have said that its nature is augmentation, because when it is with benefics, it increases their fortune; and when it is with malefics, it increases their malice. And its Firdaria years are three. Its Tail, however, is evil; and its nature is composed of the nature of Saturn and Mars; it signifies dejection and fall and poverty. And some have said that its nature signifies diminution, because when it is with benefics, it diminishes their fortune; when it is with malefics, it diminishes their malice. Therefore it is said that the Head is benefic when it is with benefics, and malefic when with malefics; and the Tail is malefic when with benefics, and benefic when with malefics. And its Firdaria years are two. Regarding the hours of the day and night, which belong to the planets. If there is any day or night of any of the planets, the first hour is of that planet, and the second hour is of the other planet that succeeds it; the succession of the others is according to the order of the circles by proportion, for example: on the day of Venus, to which the day belongs, the first hour is of Venus itself, the second of Mercury, the third of the Moon, the fourth of Saturn, the fifth of Jupiter, the sixth of Mars, the seventh of the Sun, the eighth again of Venus, the ninth of Mercury, the tenth of the Moon, the eleventh of Saturn, the twelfth of Jupiter. Behold, you have 12 unequal hours of the day. Likewise for the hours of the night. The first hour of the following night is of Mars, to which the whole night belongs. The second of the Sun. The third of Venus. The fourth of Mercury. The fifth of the Moon. The sixth of Saturn. The seventh of Jupiter. The eighth again of Mars. The ninth of the Sun. The tenth of Venus. The eleventh of Mercury. The twelfth of the Moon. And thus you also have 12 unequal hours of the night. And the day of Saturday begins afterwards, whose first hour is of Saturn; and the whole day is his. Thus by counting in order, you will find the hours of the days and nights and their divisions among the individual planets, if God wills. Regarding masculine and feminine hours. The hours are also said to be masculine and feminine, because the first hour of each day and night is masculine, the second feminine, the third masculine, the fourth feminine. Thus they succeed in order, one feminine, the other masculine, up to the end of the day and night.

[Mars, Venus, and Mercury]
to choose by color. For in this saying there is a doubt which we must resolve. For many believe that color does not show the virtue of a thing, and this is true in earthly things because of the mixture of elements that is in them. But in celestial things it is not so, because their substance is in no way composed of any element. And because of this, Ptolemy returned to proving this virtue in another way, saying: and that which exists around the Sun, and that the sphere in which the Sun is placed is below it, he wants to say that it happens that this thing is true because the virtue of Mars burns that which exists around the Sun, and that the Sun is below them, its virtue mixes with that of the Sun, it is very hot and dry, so that it burns without moderation. Daly Abenragel says Mars is a hot and dry, fiery planet, a destroyer, angry, victorious, loving to kill and slaughter, quarrels, disputes, quick to anger, sounding anger, exposing his whole body in his affairs, making battles and destroying populations. His exaltation is in the house of Saturn, that is, in Capricorn, which signifies shouts, impediments, and foolish people and wars. Saturn agrees with Mars in misfortune and resists him in coldness and darkness, inclines to the Sun for love of it and defends it with the help of its rays, because the Sun is exalted in its house and governs it with heat and dryness, and receives from it: its property and nature agree and approach the property and nature of the Sun. He is ignorant and forgetful of little intellect and diminished sense, nor does he consider the ends of things: through him and through his ascent and descent in his circle, the heat of summer and the cold of winter increase and decrease every year. Alfragan says that Mars contains the quantity of the earth one and a half and an eighth part of it. If by aspect fortune. The nature of the Sun and the letter needs no gloss. Ptolemy says it is known that the work of the substance of the Sun is to heat and to give some dryness, and these operations are felt more properly and are more easily known than all others because of the magnitude of the Sun and because of the manifest change which it makes through the seasons of the year, and the more it approaches our heads, the more it heats. Daly Abenragel says know that the Sun is the light and candle of heaven, the governor of the world, the maker of seasons: through it the planets become oriental and occidental: and through it they become apparent and hidden: and through it every moving thing moves: through it every nascent thing is known: every leaf grows and every fruit ripens. He is the great spirit of heaven, with him the signs are vivified: and every sign when it is in him has greater power over other signs. Because he vivifies and illuminates it and gives it strength and heat and applies the heat and strength and virtue of that sign to the earth: because its nature and its deeds appear in all things and in all living and inanimate things existing on earth. And when it leaves the sign in which it is, that sign remains in the likeness of a dead body. It is a planet of great dominion, power, nobility, height and magnitude. It is fortune by aspect and misfortune by bodily conjunction. For you see that when any planet joins with it: it burns and overcomes it and extinguishes its light and splendor. Its place in heaven is the fourth, that is, the middle. And of the planets: like a wise king who maintains his kingdom by sense and by consideration places his seat in the middle of his kingdom so that he may reach through all sides. He gave Mars his militia and that he should be hard in his militia: because the heaven of the Sun is below the heaven of Mars and its nature and heat agree with the nature and heat of that. He gave Jupiter his judgments because of the temperance, honesty, salvation and health of his complexion: and that there is no bad quality in him nor a nature to sin. He gave Saturn the kingdom because all planets send their lights to him and their considerations. He gave Venus the collection of revenues and the selling of revenues and buying: because its heaven applies to his and they are neighbors. He gave Mercury the scribeship: because his status is like the status of the king's scribe who goes when he goes and sits when he sits. He gave the Moon the viziership: who is like the king's vizier who does his commands and carries them wherever he commands. Alfragan says on the authority of Ptolemy that the body of the Sun contains the body of the earth sixty-six times and a little more. Venus, strong, feminine, nocturnal, here places the nature of Venus and it is clear in the letter what it says. Ptolemy says Venus herself does the works of Jupiter because of the temperance of her complexion, except that she is contrary to Jupiter in one thing: because she heats a little because she exists around the Sun and moistens according to the Moon because of the great light this planet has because it attracts to itself the smokiness that rises from the humors of the earth. Daly in his commentary wants to say that her heat is much less than that of Jupiter: and because of the humidity she makes, we say that she is somewhat cold and more humid. But what he says because she exists around the Sun, he said because her virtue is willing with that of the Sun. And what he said she moistens like the Moon: he wants to say that Venus makes humidity around her that the Moon makes. And what he said because of great light, he wants to say that little heat makes humors flow. Daly Abenragel says Venus is a cold and humid nocturnal fortune, cheerful, joyful, of good appetite, clear, beautiful: she loves embraces, songs, eating, drinking and vices: she is gentle and of little movement. She is a significator of women and of lying with them, of love, friendship and society. She receives Mars by nature of fornication and purification, she abhors him by the property of her nature which is heat and dryness. She separates herself from him and repels his evil and misfortune from herself because of her gentleness, good words, good solace, and gentle speech. She agrees with Saturn in coldness and the presence she has with him in Libra: because it is the house of one and the exaltation of the other. And she disagrees with him in morals, sadness and his sorrows and because Saturn is of little use with women. The status of Venus with the status of the Sun is similar to the status of a woman towards a man. Alfragan says that the body of Venus is one part of 37 parts of the earth. Mercury is mixed with the hypothesis and Ptolemy says: but the dryness and humidity of Mercury is by an equal one: because sometimes it dries and drives away humors because it never moves far from the heat of the Sun, also at no time, and sometimes it moistens because it is placed above the sphere of the Moon which is closer to the earth than all other spheres and changes to these two states and makes winds because of its late changes around the Sun. Daly in his commentary says. He wants to say that the work of Mercury is not one thing alone: because sometimes it dries and sometimes it moistens. But when it dries, it is when it applies to the Sun and then its work is in heating and drying around that of the Sun. But its moistening is because of its power which mixes with that of the Moon which is placed below it and its work is like the work of the Moon. And Ptolemy who makes a comparison of the work of Mercury with that of the Sun found that some made such a work as the Sun. And when he makes a comparison with the work of the Moon, he found that sometimes it made such a work as the Moon. And he experienced this many times and found that it always made one of the two works and knew for certain that its work is according to the work of the other stars with which it is involved: and it has no proper work in itself. Daly Abenragel says. Mercury is a planet of evils, violences, documents, scribeship, computations, sciences: it is hot and dry, of changeable form and nature: masculine with males: feminine with females: fortunate with fortunes: unfortunate with misfortunes: well-reasoned: eloquent, bold in speaking: of beautiful appearance: of composed person: he loves books and computations. He likes magistracies: well-done things, verified reasons, books and sciences: he is agile in movement and of ardent piety: lively and mobile in all his affairs; and he is one of the three planets.

[Almuten Calculation and Profection]
If a planet has a greater share or more strengths in the five aforementioned places, from which it receives hyleg, which are the place of the Sun, the place of the Moon, the place of conjunction or prevention, the Part of Fortune, and the degree of the Ascendant, that planet is the almuten, meaning the victor. And if any planet has dignities in one or three or more of the aforementioned places, that is the almuten. For example: I assume that one planet is the lord of the Ascendant and the lord of the terms of the same Ascendant, and with this, the lord of the face of the same. Such a planet would have 8 strengths in the Ascendant. And I assume that another planet is the lord of the exaltation of the Ascendant and the lord of the house of the Sun's place and the lord of the triplicity of the Part of Fortune. Such a planet would be more worthy as almuten than the first, because it has more strengths in the aforementioned places. And to shorten the discourse, the strengths of each planet should be collected in the five aforementioned places, and the one among them that abounds in the number of strengths will be the almuten. From this comes profection in the years of nativities and of the world. In this chapter, it teaches how profection moves from one sign to another, and this in two ways. First, in the years of nativities. Second, in the years of great conjunctions. The work in the years of nativities is easy, and the meaning of the letter is this: When you wish to know to which sign the year of profection of someone's nativity applies, see how many complete years have passed since birth, and you will begin from the ascending degree of the nativity, and you will give one sign to each year, and where the number ends, there will be the sign of profection from the Ascendant. For example: the Ascendant of someone's nativity was 10 degrees of Aries. At the end of the first year, profection comes to 10 degrees of Taurus. At the end of the second year, to 10 degrees of Gemini, and so on according to this order, giving one sign to each year until the completion of 12 years. For then, at the end of 12 years, it returns to the radical place. If, however, many years have passed since birth, subtract 12 from the total number of completed years that have passed since birth as many times as you can, that is, divide by 12, and project the number that remains below 12 from the Ascendant of the nativity according to the method previously stated. For example: the Ascendant of a certain nativity was 13 degrees of Virgo, and 32 complete solar years have passed since birth. I will subtract 12 from 32 years twice, and 8 complete years remain. I will therefore give the first year to Virgo, the second to Libra, the third to Scorpio, the fourth to Sagittarius, the fifth to Capricorn, the sixth to Aquarius, the seventh to Pisces, the eighth to Aries. The profection will then come to the sign that immediately succeeds, namely to Taurus, to a degree similar to the radical degree, namely to the 13th of the same. As I said about the ascending degree, so it must be done for the degree of the Sun, and the degree of the Moon, and the degree of the Part of Fortune. And where the year applies, the lord of that sign is the disposer of that year. And from that, the deeds in which the native will be involved in that year, and the fortunes and misfortunes that will befall him in that year, are taken. The author gives examples in the text, so it is not necessary to insist much on examples. Then the author says that when the profection of the year has reached some degree of some sign, and there is some planet or the rays of some planet after that degree, in the same sign or in the same house in the figure, and you wish to know when the profection will reach that planet or its rays: see how many degrees and minutes there are between the degree to which the year has come and that planet or its rays, and multiply them by 12 and one-sixth. This is to say, you will give to each degree 12 days and one-sixth of one, and you will find the days from the beginning of that year until the time when the profection will reach the planet or its rays. The reason why 12 days and one-sixth of one are given to each degree is that in this way, at the end of the year, one sign is completed. For if you multiply 30 degrees by 12 and one-sixth, you will get 365 days, which are the days of one year. Ptolemy says in proposition 236 of the fourth part of the Quadripartitum: "And we will know the disposition of the events of the years by taking the number of years of the nativity, and we will project them from each of the hylegical places according to the order of the signs, giving one year to each sign, and we will take the dispositor from the sign to which the number of degrees applies." Indeed, Da Ly in his commentary says that in this saying, Ptolemy wants to state that each sign disposes in one year, and thus the revolution of the sign in which the significator is will go, so that every 12 years it returns once until the end of life. All astrologers know this. Profection, however, from the years of the world. This work of profection is in the years of the world. The meaning of the letter is this: When you wish to know the application of the years of any sect, see how many complete solar years have passed from the beginning of that year in which there was a great conjunction that signified that sect, and divide that number of years by 12, and project the number that remains below 12 from the Ascendant of that year in which the conjunction occurred, and where the number applies, there is the sign of profection. The author gives an example in the text about the sect of the Saracens, i.e., Muhammad, and says that between the year of the conjunction that signified that law and the year of Muhammad's appearance, i.e., when he began to preach, there were 61 years. Another text says 52 years. I believe it should be 52 years and 57 days, otherwise it will not agree with what he says later. And the Ascendant of the year in which that conjunction occurred was the sign of Gemini, and that year in which he began to preach came to the sign of Virgo, i.e., to the sign of that planet which was the lord of the ascending sign of the year of the conjunction. For if 61 is subtracted by 12 as many times as possible, 3 remain. Therefore, the first is Gemini, the second Cancer, the third Leo, and the incomplete year that was placed in the number came to the sign of Virgo. It is not of great concern to us how many years there were from the year of that conjunction until the first year of the Arabs. It is sufficient for us to know that the year in which the Arab years began came to Virgo, because the Arab years are known to us from the tables of their extraction, and we can begin from Virgo, as the author says in the text. And because the author himself and his works were in his parts for the years of the Persians, he applies his discourse to the years of the Persians, and says: when you wish to have a brief knowledge of this matter, to know to which sign the year applies from the year of the conjunction that signified the sect of the Saracens, see how many years of the Persians have passed, convert them into days by the table of their extraction serving the years of the Persians, or multiply the years by 365, for a Persian year contains that many days, because Persian years do not have the exact day, and to the number of days that you find, add 3624 days, for that many days were from the beginning of the Arab years until the beginning of the Persian years. And what is collected, divide by 365 and one-fourth, and solar years will result. If there is any remainder, these will be the days of the imperfect year. And you can also reduce the number of days to solar years by the tables of their extraction serving the solar years. The whole intention of the author is that we know how many complete solar years have passed from the beginning of the Arab years until the time of consideration, and we give to each.

[Parts of the Third House]
There are two parts of the third house. The first is the Part of Brothers. The second is the Part of the Benevolence of Brothers. Albumazar says that the Part of Brothers and its lord, that is, the lord of the sign in which it falls, signify the existence of brothers and their concord and love, and their peregrination and absence. After this, see if this part and its lord fall in signs of many children, then the brothers will be many. And if they fall in signs of few children, they will be few. And if you wish to know their number, take the number of signs that were between the part and the lord of the house in which it fell, or how many there were between the lord and the part, and assign one to each sign. And if there is a common sign between them, double the number of that sign. And if there is any other planet between the part itself and the lord of the house in which it fell, also assign one to it. Albumazar also places one part in this house which is called the Part of the Death of Brothers, and he says that it is taken in the day from the Sun to the degree of the Midheaven, and at night the opposite. And the degrees of the Ascendant are added above, and it is projected from the Ascendant. As often as this part comes by direction to the significators of brothers and sisters, giving one year to each degree, or by perfection, giving a year to each sign, something horrible will happen to the brothers and sisters, or some of them will die. The Fourth House. Here are placed the parts of the fourth house, and there are five. The first is the Part of Fathers. The second is the Part of the Death of the Father. The third is the Part of Years. The fourth is the Part of Inheritances and Possessions. The fifth is the Part of the Nobility of the Native, whether he is the son of him to whom he is assigned or not. The sixth is the Part of the Lord of Things. Albumazar says that the Part of the Father signifies the existence of the father and his nobility and lineage. And if this part is of good essence, the father will be noble. And if the lord of the house of this part is of good essence, the father will be fortunate. But if it is of bad essence, he will be laborious. From the second part of this house, which is the Part of the Death of the Father, the cause of death is taken. As often as the perfection of the year comes to this part or to its lord, it signifies danger to the father. And if any of them come to the significators of the father. The Fifth House. Here are placed the parts of the fifth house, and there are seven. The first is the Part of Children. The second is the Part of the Time in which children should be had. The third is the Part by which masculinity or femininity is known. The fourth is the Part by which it is known concerning the native about whom the question is asked, whether he is male or female. The fifth is the Part to which, when Jupiter comes, it is a signification of a child. The sixth is the Part of the Love of Children. The seventh is the Part of the Knowledge of Children. Albumazar says that if the Part of Children falls in a sign of many children, he will have many children. But if it falls in a sterile sign, he will not have any child. But if it falls in a sign of few children, he will have few children. And if this part signifies children and is fortunate, the children will live. And if unfortunate, they will die. The Sixth House. Here are placed the parts of the sixth house, and there are two. The first is the Part of Azemena, that is, the inseparable debility of some member. The second is the Part of Servants. If the Part of Azemena is conjoined with benefics, the native will be healthy in his members. But if it is conjoined with malefics, he will have inseparable diseases in his members. And the places where these diseases will be are known from the places of the malefics signifying them. Here are placed the parts of the seventh house, and there are four. The first is the Part of the Betrothal of Men. The second is the Part of the Betrothal of Women. And this is taken in two ways. The third is of Delight and Pleasure. The fourth is the Part of Marriages. When the Part of Betrothal comes by direction to Jupiter or Venus, it is a signification of betrothal. And I found in one nativity the time of betrothal when the lord of the Part of Betrothal came to that part by direction, giving one year to each degree. The Eighth House. Here are placed the parts of the eighth house, and there are four. The first is the Part of Death. The second is the Part of the Planet that kills. The third is the Part of the Year in which death or poverty will come to the native. The fourth is the Part of Prevention and Litigation. Here Albumazar says that if the Part of Death is impeded and its lord, and benefics do not aspect them, the native will die a most shameful death. But if benefics aspect them, it will be the opposite. If the Moon or Sun aspects the Part of the Killing Planet, and the Moon itself is in a sign of amputated members, the native will die by suffering. And if the Moon is impeded, something will be cut off from his members. When the Part of the Year in which death is feared for the native and its lord, with the lord of the Ascendant, are impeded, the native will be of many infirmities and affliction in body and substance, and will often approach the loss of body and substance. And as often as the perfection of the year comes to this part, or this part comes by perfection or direction to the Ascendant or to its lord, the native will find dangers in body and infirmities, and will find distress and horror in substance. He will also fear death from various parts. The Ninth House. Here are placed the parts of the ninth house, and there are two. The first is the Part of Peregrination. The second is the Part of Travel by Water. From these are taken the peregrinations of the native and travels by water. Albumazar says: If the Part of Travel by Water falls in an aquatic sign, the native will make many travels by water, and if it is fortunate there, he will have profit and gain in his travels. And if it is unfortunate, it signifies the opposite. The Tenth House. Here are placed the parts of the tenth house, and there are five. The first is the Part of Kings and Kingdom. The second is the Part of the King and Kingdom. The third is the Part of Principalities of the Kingdom. The fourth is the Part signifying whether it is the cause of the kingdom or not. The fifth is the Part of Mothers. The Eleventh House. Here are placed the parts of the eleventh house, and there are two. The first is the Part of Friends. The second is the Part signifying the profit and effect and friendship of friends. Here is placed only one part of the Twelfth House, that of enemies. And these are other parts that the masters of judgments use. Here are placed some other parts that are not in any of the houses, and there are six. The first is the Part of False Rumor. The second is the Part of Reason and Profundity of Sense. The third is the Part of Wisdom and Discipline. The fourth is the Part of War and Battles. The fifth is the Part of Patience. The sixth is the Part of Aspecting in the Revolution of Years. And all these are projected from the Ascendant. And because, with God's help, the author first placed the parts that fall in nativities. Here he places the parts that fall in the revolutions of the years of the world. And it can be divided into two parts: because first he places the parts that the masters of judgments use in revolutions in the causes of kingdoms. And he places the parts that the masters of judgments use in knowing the future of things. The second is there. Also, there are other parts here. He says that from the parts that are exercised in the revolutions of the years of the world to know the causes of the kingdom and empire, and this is taken from Mars to the Moon, and is projected from the Ascendant of the conjunction that signifies the change of the kingdom, and is taken in another way from the degree of the Ascendant of the conjunction to the degree of the conjunction, understanding from the degree of the Ascendant of the revolution of the year to the degree of the conjunction.

[Introduction to Astrological Judgments]
Alchabitius with commentary. With grace and privilege. Horizon B 8 II circular. Circle of Cancer. Equinoctial. Circle of Capricorn. Circle of Antarctic. Zenith oblique. The Isagogic Book of Abdilazi, that is, the servant of the glorious God, who is called Alchabitius, for the mastery of astrological judgments, interpreted by John of Seville, and a commentary on the same by John of Saxony, connected in a useful series, begin. Having sought from the Lord the longevity of Cephas Dala, that is, the sword of the kingdom and the durability of his honor, and also the custody of his works, whether good or bad, and the extension of his empire, let us begin what we wish to narrate. When I saw that some ancient authors of the mastery of astrological judgments had published books which they called introductory to this mastery, that is, of astrological judgments, but some of them had not diligently investigated all that is necessary in the same mastery concerning those things which are suitable for an introduction. And some indeed had presented what is necessary at length, and because I perceived that what is necessary in it had perished. And also, when I observed that some had not proceeded in the path of discipline in the arrangement of what they presented, I began to publish this book, and I made it an introduction. And I collected in it from the sayings of the ancients whatever is necessary for this mastery according to the introductory method, and I did not introduce the reasonings of disputation or defense of what we presented as necessary, since they are in Ptolemy's book which is called Alarbamacalet, that is, of four treatises, and in my book which I published in confirmation of the mastery of astrological judgments in the destruction of the epistle of Baissibenbali, in its annulment by reasoning which can suffice for this. And I divided it into five differences. The first difference is in the essential and accidental being of the circle of signs. The second difference is in the natures of the seven planets, what is proper to them, and what they signify. The third difference is in those things which happen to the seven planets in themselves, and what happens to them mutually. The fourth difference is in the exposition of astrological names. The fifth difference is in the universality of the parts and the exposition of their being in degrees. First difference. Concerning the division of the circle of signs. The zodiac, that is, the circle of signs, is divided into twelve equal parts according to the division of the circle of signs. And these twelve parts are called signs and refer to the images which are under the same zodiacal circle. They are Aries, Taurus, Gemini, Cancer, Leo, Virgo, Libra, Scorpio, Sagittarius, Capricorn, Aquarius, Pisces. And each of these signs is divided into thirty equal parts, called degrees. And a degree is divided into sixty minutes, and minutes into sixty seconds, and seconds into sixty thirds. Similarly, fourths and fifths follow, ascending to infinity. And six of these signs are northern, that is, from the beginning of Aries to the end of Virgo, and they are northern from the equinoctial line. And six are southern, that is, from the beginning of Libra to the end of Pisces. And six of them are called direct ascending, that is, from the beginning of Cancer to the end of Sagittarius. And six are called tortuous ascending, that is, from the beginning of Capricorn to the end of Gemini. And the tortuous ascending signs obey the direct ascending signs. That is, two signs which are of the same longitude from the head of Cancer obey each other, such as Gemini to Cancer, Taurus to Leo, Aries to Virgo. And Pisces to Libra, Aquarius to Scorpio, and Capricorn to Sagittarius. And two signs which are of the same longitude from the head of Aries are said to be in agreement in their path, such as Aries and Pisces, Taurus and Aquarius, Gemini and Capricorn, Cancer and Sagittarius, Leo and Scorpio, Virgo and Libra. And the half of the circle from the beginning of Leo to the end of Capricorn is called the greater half, and it is the half of the Sun, because the Sun has principality in all this half, just as the planets have in their terms. And the other half, which is from the beginning of Aquarius to the end of Cancer, is called the lesser half, and it is the half of the Moon, because the Moon similarly has principality in all this half, just as the Sun in the greater half. And that half which is from the beginning of Aries to the end of Virgo is called the hot half. And the other, which is from the beginning of Libra to the end of Pisces, is called the cold half. And that fourth part of the circle which is from the beginning of Aries to the end of Gemini is called the hot, humid, vernal, youthful, sanguine quarter. And that which is from the beginning of Cancer to the end of Virgo is called the hot, dry, aestival, adolescent, choleric quarter. And that which is from the beginning of Libra to the end of Sagittarius is called the cold, dry, autumnal, melancholic quarter, and it signifies the beginning of the diminution of middle age. And that which is from the beginning of Capricorn to the end of Pisces is called the cold, humid, defective, senile, hibernal, phlegmatic quarter. All the planets which are carried in these signs are not in them, but because they are carried under them, that is, in their direction. Higher and closer to the circle of signs and slower in course is Saturn, then Jupiter, then Mars, then the Sun, then Venus, then Mercury, then the Moon, which is closer to the Earth and faster in course than all. Certain significations are also indicated by the head of the Dragon and the tail with the planets, as we will explain in the following. Concerning the houses of the planets. The planets have powers in these signs, some by nature, some by accident. Those which are by nature are these: houses, exaltation, term, triplicity, face. We will treat of those which are by accident in a suitable place. The houses are these: Aries and Scorpio, house of Mars. Taurus and Libra, house of Venus. Gemini and Virgo, house of Mercury. Cancer, house of the Moon. Leo, house of the Sun. Sagittarius and Pisces, house of Jupiter. Capricorn and Aquarius, house of Saturn. The seventh sign from the house of each planet is said to be its detriment. And if two signs are the house of one planet, they are said to be in agreement in the almantica, that is, in the circle which is wide in the middle and narrow at the ligature, it signifies the zodiacal circle. The signs in which the planets are said to rejoice when they enter, and their lords according to Dorotheus, are these: Saturn is said to rejoice when he enters Aquarius. Jupiter in Sagittarius. Mars in Scorpio. Venus in Taurus. And Mercury in Virgo. Concerning the exaltations of the planets. These are the exaltations of the planets: The Sun is exalted in Aries, that is, in its 18th degree. The Moon in the 3rd degree of Taurus. Saturn in the 21st of Libra. Jupiter in the 15th degree of Cancer. Mars in the 28th degree of Capricorn. Venus in the 27th degree of Pisces. Mercury in the 15th of Virgo. The Head of the Dragon in the 3rd degree of Gemini. And the Tail in the 3rd degree of Sagittarius. In the seventh sign from the exaltation of each planet, in a similar degree will be its fall. For example, just as the Sun is exalted in the 18th degree of Aries, so it falls in the 18th degree of Libra, and so for the others. Ptolemy, however, places the whole of Aries as the exaltation of the Sun. And the whole of Taurus as the exaltation of the Moon, and so on for the others. Concerning triplicities. We distinguish triplicities thus: Three signs which appear to agree in one nature form a triplicity and are called by the same name, that is, triplicity. Therefore, Aries, Leo, and Sagittarius form the first triplicity, because each of these signs is fiery, masculine, diurnal, hot, and dry, choleric, bitter in taste. This triplicity is also oriental. Its lords are the Sun by day and Jupiter by night, and their participant by day and night is Saturn. The second triplicity is from Taurus, Virgo, and Capricorn, because these are feminine, nocturnal, earthy, cold, and dry, melancholic, acrid in taste, southern signs. The lords of this triplicity are Venus by day and the Moon by night, whose participant by day and night is Mars. The third triplicity is from Gemini, Libra, and Aquarius, because these signs are masculine, diurnal, sanguine, hot, humid, airy, sweet in taste, western. The lords of this triplicity are Saturn by day and Mercury by night, among whom Jupiter is the participant by day and night. The fourth triplicity is formed by Cancer, Scorpio, and Pisces, because these are feminine, nocturnal, northern, watery, phlegmatic, cold, humid, salty in taste. The lords of this triplicity are by day...

[Direction of Significators]
When you know the significator and wish to know where the direction will arrive from the circle of signs in a certain number of years, if the significator is in the ascendant, add the number of years to the ascensions of the degree of the ascendant, and make that arc in the ascensions of the region. Where the arc of degrees from the circle of signs ends, there the direction will arrive in that same year. If the significator is in the 7th house, add the number of years to the ascensions of the nadir of the significator's degree, and arc this also in the ascensions of the region. Where it ends from the circle of signs, the direction will arrive at its nadir in the same year. If the significator is in the 10th or 4th house, add the number of years to the ascensions of the significator's degree in the direct circle, and arc it in the ascensions of the direct circle. Where it ends from the circle of signs, there the direction will arrive in the same year. If the significator is outside these four places, which are the angles, you must know the hours of longitude from the angle as I said before. If the significator is in the eastern half, add the number of years you wish to the ascensions of the significator's degree through the direct circle, and arc this in the ascensions of the direct circle. What results will be the significator of the direct circle; keep it. After this, add the number of years also to the ascensions of the significator's degree in the region, and arc this in the ascensions of the region. What results will be the significator of the region. After this, take the sixth part of the remainder between the significator of the direct circle and the significator of the region, and multiply it by the hours of longitude from the angle. What results will be the equation. If the significator of the direct circle is less than the significator of the region, add the equation to the significator of the direct circle. If it is more, subtract it from it. What remains there is where the direction will arrive from the circle of signs in the same year. If the significator is in the western half, do with the nadir of the significator's degree as you did with the significator's degree in the operation before it. What results there is where the direction will arrive from the circle of signs in the same year. The place to which the direction arrives is called the place of division, and the lord of the term of that place is called the divisor. If another planet or its rays or a place near it is in the degree of division, this planet or the lord of the rays is said to be a participant of the divisor in the division. The significators that are directed are five places: the degree of the ascendant, the degree of the Sun, the degree of the Moon, the degree of the Part of Fortune, and the degree of the Midheaven. The degree of the ascendant is directed to discern accidents that happen to the body. The degree of the Sun is for causes of dignity and exaltation, honor, and kingdom. The Moon is for the being of the soul and body and marriage. The Part of Fortune is for acquisitions and progress, scarcity and abundance. The Midheaven is for mastery and other particular dispositions and their being. If the ascendant of a revolution of any world years or nativities is directed, its significators are directed according to this direction, namely, one day for each degree. Some believe that the significators of the year are directed in this way for all: namely, 59 minutes and 8 seconds for one day. For the direction of kings and princes is directed to them from the degree of the Midheaven through the ascensions of the direct circle, 56 minutes and 8 seconds for one day, until it reaches good or bad planets. And the being of kings in health or illness is directed from the degree of the ascendant to good or bad planets, 59 minutes and 8 seconds for one day through the ascensions of the region. The direction in the revolution of world years and to predict the being of the common people or rustics is from the degree of the ascendant, similarly to predict the being of the king from the degree of the Midheaven. And in the revolution of nativity years, to predict the being of the native from the degree of the ascendant of the revolution, 59 minutes and 8 seconds for one day through the ascensions of the region. Concerning Algebugthar. The law of Algebugthar in nativities is the direction of the degree of the ascendant. This means that you look at the degree of the ascendant in whose term it is, and subtract the ascensions of the ascendant from the ascensions that are in the direct end of the planet's term through the ascensions of the region. For what remains, you take one year for each degree, and one month for every five minutes, and 6 days for every minute. The lord of the term will be the disposer of the years, which is called the divisor. After this, take the degrees of the term that succeeds it, and convert them also into degrees of ascensions. For what results, take one year for each degree, and one month for every 5 minutes, and six days for every minute. The lord of the term will be the divisor and disposer of those years. Similarly, you will enter with every term of the lord by succession until the end of life. If it is in the term of any planet, the planet or its rays will be participants in the division. This division is called Algebugthar. Concerning the Duodenaries of Planets and Houses. The law of the duodenaries of planets or houses means that you look at how much the planet has moved in its sign, in whatever sign it is, or the degree of the house you wish, in degrees and minutes. You will multiply this by 12. After this, add to it the degrees and minutes that you multiplied by 12. What is collected from it, project from the beginning of the degree of the same sign, giving 30 degrees to each sign. Where the number ends, there will be the duodenary of the planets and houses. Concerning their Novenaries. The law of Amanbabarat, which are the novenaries. The knowledge of this is to know how much the planet has moved in its sign in degrees and minutes, or the degree of the house whose novenary you wish to know. After this, divide the sign into nine divisions, and each division is three degrees and a third part of one degree. After this, look in which novenary out of the novenaries the degree of the planet or house falls. After this, give the first novenary from the signs to the lord of the movable sign of the same triplicity, and the second novenary to the lord of the sign of which it is itself.

[On the Terms of the Planets]
The terms or bounds of the planets in the signs are those where, in each sign, certain planets have terms arranged through different degrees. From the beginning of Aries up to the sixth degree of the same Aries is the term of Jupiter. From the sixth up to the twelfth is the term of Venus. From the twelfth up to the twentieth is the term of Mercury. From the twentieth to the twenty-fifth is the term of Mars and Saturn. Due to the diversity of their degrees and the difficulty of remembering them, we have described them in a table so that the work may be easier. The Egyptian terms are said to be these: 6 9 8 5 6 5 6 5 7 3 6 1 7 4 6 5 8 7 6 7 6 7 9 6 7 4 7 4 14 6 9 5 7 6 7 6 7 10 7 0 4 7 2 6 8 8 7 7 9 7 2 7 9 4 8 2 0 5 6 1 0 7 7 4 1 2 9 5 8 4 6 5 4 17 7 4 17 8 6 4 4 7 9 16 2 7 5 6 5 12 20 4 3 9 6 2.

[When Triplicities are Preferred to Terms]
Some prefer triplicities to terms because the lords of triplicities are stronger in nourishment, as they signify nourishment, and because there is no discord in a triplicity, as there is in terms when they are preferred. And some prefer terms to triplicities because the lords of terms are stronger in direction.

[On the Faces of the Signs and to Which Planets They are Attributed]
The faces of the signs are these: each sign is divided into three equal parts. Each part consists of ten degrees and is called a face, the beginning of which is from the first degree of Aries. Therefore, the first face is from the first degree of Aries up to the tenth, and it is given to Mars. The second up to the twentieth degree is given to the Sun, who succeeds him in the order of the circles. The third up to the end of the aforesaid sign is of Jupiter. Similarly, the first face of Taurus is of Mercury, who succeeds Venus, and so on to the end of the signs. Therefore, when you have a degree in any sign and wish to know to which planet's face it belongs, take the whole signs from the beginning of Aries up to the sign you wish to know about, and triple it. And what remains, add to what has passed from the faces of that sign about which you wish to know the face, with the same face whose lord you wish to know. And project from the planet who is the lord of the face of the sign of Aries, who is Mars, according to the succession of the circles. And what remains within seven, count from Mars according to the succession of the planets. And where the number ends, that will be the first face of that sign, from which the degree was, up to the tenth of that sign, of the planet at whom the number ends. And from the tenth up to the twentieth, of the other planet who succeeds him. And from the twentieth up to the end, of the other sign who succeeds him. And in whose tenth the degree is from the sign, that will be the face of that planet. The lords of these faces are also called decans by some, whose table follows: In Aries 10 Mars, 10 Sun, 10 Jupiter. In Taurus 10 Venus, 10 Mercury, 10 Saturn. In Gemini 10 Jupiter, 10 Mars, 10 Sun. In Cancer 10 Venus, 10 Mercury, 10 Saturn. In Leo 10 Jupiter, 10 Mars, 10 Sun. In Virgo 10 Venus, 10 Mercury, 10 Saturn. In Libra 10 Jupiter, 10 Mars, 10 Sun. In Scorpio 10 Venus, 10 Mercury, 10 Saturn. In Sagittarius 10 Jupiter, 10 Mars, 10 Sun. In Capricorn 10 Venus, 10 Mercury, 10 Saturn. In Aquarius 10 Jupiter, 10 Mars, 10 Sun. In Pisces 10 Venus, 10 Mercury, 10 Saturn.

[On the Virtues of the Planets]
Since, by God's grace, we have now discussed the powers of the planets in the signs, which are their house, exaltation, triplicity, term, and face, let us now discuss their virtues or strengths within themselves. For the lord of the house has 5 strengths, the lord of the exaltation 4, the lord of the triplicity 3, the lord of the term 2, and the lord of the face 1. Understand, therefore, from these numbers the strengths of the planets. For those that abound more in number, abound more in strength. And some prefer the term to the triplicity, that is, they want the lord of the term to be stronger than the lord of the triplicity. But we have already explained above in what respect one is valid. Some also have given such a comparison concerning this matter, saying that when a planet is in its house, it is like a man in his own house and in his own dominion. And when it is in its exaltation, it is like a man in his kingdom and glory. And when it is in its term, it is like a man among his parents and relatives and people. And when it is in its triplicity, it will be like a man in his honor and among his helpers and ministers. And when it is in its face, it will be like a man in his magistracy. These are all the essential powers of the planets in the signs, and the figures of the signs follow these.

[On the Essences of the Signs and What They Signify in Themselves]
Among the signs, there are some signs that are called human, namely Virgo, Gemini, Libra, and Aquarius, and the first half of Sagittarius, because their images in the circle are figured as images of humans. These are also called signs having beautiful voices. These are also strong when they are in the East. And some are said to have wings, namely Gemini, Virgo, and Pisces. And some are quadrupedal, like Leo and Sagittarius. Some of them are domestic, like Aries, Taurus, and Capricorn, and these are strong when they are in the South. But Virgo, Capricorn, and Aquarius are strong when they are in the North. And among the signs, some are entirely fruitful and some are vicious, namely Aries, Taurus, Cancer, Scorpio, and Capricorn. And some of them are said to have many offspring, namely Cancer, Scorpio, and Pisces. And these are strong when they are in the West. And some of them are sterile, like Gemini, Leo, and Virgo. And some have few children, like Aries, Taurus, Libra, Sagittarius, Capricorn, and Aquarius. And some are said to be very luxurious, namely Aries, Taurus, Leo, and Capricorn. And among the signs, some are said to have a medium voice and are formed in the images of bleating, lowing, and roaring animals, like Aries, Taurus, Leo, and Capricorn, and the last part of Sagittarius. And some are voiceless, namely those that are formed in the images of voiceless animals, namely Cancer, Scorpio, and Pisces.

[On the Significations of the Signs]
Each sign has its own significations in what it signifies concerning the created members and customs of men, and regions, and seeds, and trees, and so on. Aries has from the body of man the head and face, and from regions, Babylon, and Syria, that is, Babylonia and Persia and Arabia and Philistia and Palestine. Taurus has trees that are planted, and from the body of man it has the neck and the knot of the throat, and from regions, Egypt and Almechim and Sande and Araterad. Gemini is a sign of a generous good spirit and has from the body of man the shoulders and arms and hands, and from regions, Vigeti and Armenia, Nutbrabige and Telenimstet, that is, Egypt and Bartha. Cancer has from trees those that are equal in length, and from the body of man the chest, heart, stomach, ribs, spleen, and lung, and from regions, Lesser Armenia and the eastern region of Buthabe and Masse and Acin, and it has participation in Barach and Atrabicen. Leo has tall trees, that is, long, hot, and cunning, and much distress and sadness, and from the body of man the stomach, heart, back, side, and from regions, Artitri up to the end of the habitable region. Virgo has whatever is sown from seeds, and is generous of good spirit, and has from the body of man the belly and internal parts, that is, the diaphragm and intestines, and from regions, arguments and Bum Moga Agility, Libra, that is, a certain region around Jerusalem and Alforas, that is, the Euphrates, and the island which is Hispania and Festiruel Aseum. Libra has tall trees and is generous of good spirit, and has from the body of man the loins and lower belly, navel, and groin, and genitals, hips, and buttocks, and from regions, the land of the Romans or Greeks and those adjacent to them up to Africa; it also has Arasse or Azim up to the end of Ethiopia and Barthan; it also has Carmen and Sesgestem and Thebes or Thebil and Tabrasten, Barab, and Ambarath. Scorpio has trees of equal length, generous of good spirit, and has from the body of man the genitals, testicles, bladder, anus, and thighs, and from regions, Belebiget and the lands of the Arabs and its borders up to Allegem; and it has participation in Alcbach. Sagittarius is ingenious and hot, has from the body of man the thighs, and from regions, Ethiopia and Maharabem and Achiut or Acenit or Achichit, which is India. Capricorn is of good life, irascible, cautious, and hot, having much sadness, has from the body of man the knees, and from regions, Ethiopia, Annaban, Alcon, and Acuith and Mahabem up to the two seas and Abant and Achuit, which is India. Aquarius has from the body of man the legs up to the lower ankles, that is, the heels, and from regions, Azenes, that is, blackness, and Althupha and its parts, and the land of Elfies and part of the land of Egypt and the western region and the land of Achiut. Pisces is hot and cautious, mixed with many colors, having from the body of man the feet; and from regions, Carabzarem and the northern region of the land of Jurjem and participation in the Romans up to Essen, it has an island and Egypt and Alexandria and the Lycian Sea.

[On the Signification of Planets in Signs by Members of the Body]
Indeed, when planets signify pain, they have a proper member in each sign. Let us therefore discuss the pains of the planets in the signs: and first let us begin with Aries. Saturn in Aries has the chest. Jupiter the belly. Mars the head. The Sun the thighs. Venus the feet. Mercury the legs. The Moon...

[On Pit Degrees]
In the signs there are certain degrees which are called pits: when a planet is in any of them, it is said to be in a pit, such as the sixth degree of Aries, etc., as will be shown in the following table. Aries: 6, 11, 16, 23, 29. Taurus: 8, 15, 21, 24, 25. Gemini: 2, 12, 17, 26. Cancer: 20, 30. Leo: 22, 23, 28. Virgo: 6, 12, 17, 23, 26. Libra: 8, 13, 15. Scorpio: 8, 13, 15, 21, 25. Sagittarius: 17, 20, 30. Capricorn: 9, 10, 22, 23, 27. Aquarius: 1, 17, 21, 25. Pisces: 12, 24, 27, 30.

[On Azemena Degrees (Debility of Body)]
There are in the signs certain degrees which are called Azemena degrees, that is, degrees of bodily debility.
